***hiel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hiel.html>hiel</a> (26208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hiele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:hela.html>hela</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanhilaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiel.html>hiel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hielen.html>hielen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiel.html>hieltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a>, part of the foot</li>
<li>analogous part of footwear or another physical entity</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiel.html>hiel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:likker.html>likker</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">licker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***hier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> (32)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hē₂r</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>here</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> this</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">here</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***hiernamaals.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a> (10412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hiernamaels</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hereafter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">namaals</i>. Originally an adverb.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaalsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaalsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">afterlife</span>, life after death</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hiernumaals</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hereafter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">afterwards</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of or relating to the afterlife.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hiernamaals.html>hiernamaals</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a>

***hij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> (15)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:hie.html>hie</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hē</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><i>Third-person singular, masculine, subjective:</i> he.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:loopt.html>loopt</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>He</b> walks.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>When the word occurs other than as the first word of a clause and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not emphatically stressed, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually pronounced as <span class="IPA">/i/</span>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a completely accepted pronunciation in standard speech.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Persoonlijk_voornaamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:persoonlijk.html>Persoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornaamwoord.html>voornaamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:mannelijk.html>mannelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:derde.html>derde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enkelvoud.html>enkelvoud</a> <i>nominatief</i>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a>.</i> </li>

***hijsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hijsen.html>hijsen</a> (12458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hisen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hischen</i>. Further etymology uncertain, but possibly related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hatjaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hunt down, pursue, persecute, attack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Or, possibly imitative.
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">hissen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hissen</i>.
</p>

***hil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hil</a> (64763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hil</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hille</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hulliz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stone, rock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kolən-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*koləm-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">top, hill, rock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hill</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hullen.html>hulle</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">hull</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">hóll</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">holm</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hil</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hillen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hil.html>hilletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***hilltop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a> (92504)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hill</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">top</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hilltops</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The peak or crest of a hill.
<ul><li><b>1946</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bertrand_Russell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bertrand Russell">Bertrand Russell</a>, <i>History of Western Philosophy</i>, I.21:
<dl><dd>The territory should be small enough to be surveyed in its entirety from a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>used attributively in phrases such as "a <a href = vnd.unilang:hilltop.html>hilltop</a> house"</li></ul>
</body>

***hinken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hinken.html>hinken</a> (54291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hinken.html>hinken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hinkan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hinkaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hinken.html>hinken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to limp, to hobble (walk with difficulty due to injury)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***hippocampus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a> (51704)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱππόκαμπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hippókampos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from
<i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ῐ̔́ππος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">híppos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κάμπος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kámpos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sea-monster</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The anatomy sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> so named from its resemblance to the seahorse.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hippocampi</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mythological creature with the front head and forelimbs of a horse and the rear of a dolphin.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">hippocamp</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A part of the brain located inside the temporal lobe, consisting mainly of grey matter. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a component of the limbic system and plays a role in memory and emotion.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">neuroanatomy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> HIPP</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hippocampal</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">hippocampic</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hippocampus.html>hippocampus</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:anatomie.html>anatomie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hersenen.html>hersenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:betrokken.html>betrokken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geheugen.html>geheugen</a>, stress <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> ruimtelijke orriëntatie

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>historie</a> (10730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>historie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">historia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱστορία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">historía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:historisch.html>historisch</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:historicus.html>historicus</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἱστορικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">historikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form borrowed from German replaced earlier forms ending on the equivalent of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hitte.html>hitte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hitta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hitjō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hitze</i>. Now commonly interpreted as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***hive.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a> (11154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hyfe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hȳf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hūbī</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">huif</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beehive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Danish dialect <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">huv</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ship’s hull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*KuHp-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water vessel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cūpa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tub, <a href = vnd.unilang:vat.html>vat</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύπη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúpē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gap, hole</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύπελλον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúpellon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beaker.html>beaker</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कूप</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kū́pa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, curve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The computing term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> chosen as an in-joke relating to bees; see <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://blogs.msdn.com/b/oldnewthing/archive/2003/08/08/54618.aspx">[1]</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A structure, whether artificial or natural, for housing a swarm of honeybees.
<ul><li><b>1709</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Works_of_Virgil_(Dryden)/Georgics_(Dryden)" class="extiw" title="s:The Works of Virgil (Dryden)/Georgics (Dryden)">Georgics</a></i> IV.10-13:
<dl><dd><i>First, for thy Bees a quiet Station find,</i></dd>
<dd>And lodge 'em under Covert of the Wind:</dd>
<dd>For <a href = vnd.unilang:winds.html>Winds</a>, when homeward they return, will drive</dd>
<dd>The loaded <a href = vnd.unilang:carriers.html>Carriers</a> from their Ev'<a href = vnd.unilang:ning.html>ning</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>Hive</a></b>.<i></i></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>The bees of one <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>; a swarm of bees.
<ul><li><b>c. 1602</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Troilus_and_Cressida" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Troilus and Cressida">Troilus and Cressida</a></i>, Act I, Scene iii:
<dl><dd>When that the general <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not like the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b>, to whom the foragers shall all repair, what honey <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> expected?</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A place swarming with busy occupants; a crowd.
<ul><li><b>?</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Tennyson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alfred Tennyson">Alfred Tennyson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Boadicea" class="extiw" title="s:Boadicea">Boadicea</a></i>
<dl><dd>There the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> of Roman liars worship a gluttonous emperor-idiot.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A section of the registry.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Jean Andrews,  <cite>Fixing <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> XP</cite>, page 352:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> builds the registry from the five registry <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, Samuel Phung, <i>Professional Microsoft <a href = vnd.unilang:windows.html>Windows</a> Embedded CE 6.0</i>
<dl><dd>For devices built with hive-based registry implementation, the registry data are broken into three different <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b> — the <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>, system <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>, and user <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">beehive</span></li>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mother-hive</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hives.html>hives</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hiving</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">hived</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To enter or possess a <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form a hive-like entity.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To collect into a <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a>.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> a swarm of bees</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To store in a <a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a> or similarly.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>181</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Byron" class="extiw" title="w:Lord Byron">Lord Byron</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Childe_Harold%27s_Pilgrimage" class="extiw" title="w:Childe Harold | s Pilgrimage"><a href = vnd.unilang:chillen.html>Childe</a> Harold’s Pilgrimage. </a></cite>, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Murray_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:John Murray (publisher)">John Murray</a>,, canto 3<span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(please specify the stanza number)</span>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd><b>Hiving</b> wisdom with each studious year.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take shelter or lodgings together; to reside in a collective body.
<ul><li><b>1596-97</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Merchant_of_Venice" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Merchant of Venice">The Merchant of Venice</a></i>, Act II, Scene v<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=merchantveniceamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[2]</a></sup>:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:shylock.html>Shylock</a>:</dd>
<dd>The patch <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> enough, but a huge feeder,</dd>
<dd>Snail-slow in profit, and he <a href = vnd.unilang:sleeps.html>sleeps</a> by day</dd>
<dd>More than the wild-cat; <a href = vnd.unilang:drones.html>drones</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> not with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>;</dd>
<dd>Therefore I part with him; and part with him</dd>
<dd>To one what I would have him help to waste</dd>
<dd>His borrowed purse. <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1725</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pope" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Pope">Alexander Pope</a>, letter to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martha_Blount" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Martha Blount">Martha Blount</a>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>to get into <a href = vnd.unilang:warmer.html>warmer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a>, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hive.html>hive</a></b> together in cities</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hockeyen.html>hockeyen</a> (39443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hockey</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hockeyen.html>hockeyen</a></strong>
</p>
